# 2025-12-24_OMEGA_Part6 QuestHub Expansion

## QST-5000: Cleanse bog idols
- **Type:** Repeatable
- **Region:** Emberford_Marketwalk
- **Objectives:** Craft 2 components
- **Rewards:** Map clue + key
- **Notes:** Introduces a mini-boss
